<S n="3000">
<s>drAkzArasasamA bAlA taruRI SarkaropamA .</s>
<s>AmrarasasamA prOQA vfdDA strI nAlikeravat ..</s>
</S>
<D n="3000">
<b>3000.</b> Ein unerwachsenes Mädchen
gleicht dem Traubensaft, eine Jungfrau
dem Zucker, eine Frau mittleren Alters
dem Safte der Mangofrucht, ein altes
Weib einer Kokosnuss.
</D>
<F n="3000">
3000) SUBHĀṢ. 24. ²b.

<s>nAnikeravat</s> die Hdschr.
</F>

<S n="3001">
<s>drumodBavaM hanti vizaM nahi drumaM na vA BujaMgapraBavaM BujaMgamam .</s>
<s>adaH samutpattipadaM dahatyaho dAholbaRaM kroDahalAhalaM mahat ..</s>
</S>
<D n="3001">
<b>3001.</b> Gift, das vom Baume kommt,
tödtet ja nicht den Baum, eben so wenig
Gift, das von der Schlangen kommt, die
Schlangen; jenes heftige und brennende
Gift des Zornes aber versengt seltsamer
Weise die Stätte, aus der es hervorging.
</D>
<F n="3001">
3001) SUBHĀṢ. 115. ²d.

<S n="3002">

<s>suryendudrohakfdrAhoH SIrzacCedo 'Bavanna kim ..</s>

<D n="3002">
<b>3002.</b> Wer Hochstehenden zu schaden

Mond anfeindete, das Haupt abgeschlagen?
</D>

<s>°kfdvAhuH</s> die Hdschr.

<S n="3003">

Obdach hat.
</D>

</S>
<D n="3004" a="4227">
<b>3004.</b> (<b>4227.</b>) Der feingebildete Mann
trete, auch wenn ihn Niemand zurückhält,
nicht in's Gemach (des Fürsten), wenn
dieser in einem Zwiegespräch begriffen
ist, oder Arzenei bei der Mahlzeit
einnimmt, oder mit den Frauen vereint
ist, oder dann, wenn der Barbier bei ihm
ist.
</D>

<S n="3077">
<s>DanyAnAM girikandarezu vasatAM jyotiH paraM DyAyatA-</s>
<s>mAnandASrukaRAnpibanti SakunA niHSaNkamaNke sTitAH .</s>
<s>asmAkaM tu manoraToparacitaprAsAdavApItawa-</s>
<s>krIqAkAnanakelikOtukajuzAmAyuH paraM kzIyate ..</s>
</S>
<D n="3077" a="1307">
<b>3077.</b> (<b>1307.</b>) Vögel sitzen furchtlos
auf dem Schoosse der Glücklichen, die,
in Bergeshöhlen wohnend, mit ihren
Gedanken in das höchste Licht (das
Brahman) sich vertieft haben, und
schlürfen die durch die höchste Wonne
erzeugten Thränentropfen; uns dagegen
schwindet nur das Leben dahin im Genuss
von Palästen, Teichufern, Lusthainen,
Spielen und Festlichkeiten, die die
Phantasie uns vorzaubert.
</D>
<F n="3077">
3077) BHARTṚ. ed. BOHL. 3, 15. HAEB.
lith. Ausg. I und GALAN. 14. ŚĀRṄG.
PADDH. ŚĀNTIŚ. 1, 5 bei HAEB. 411.
²a. <s>DaRyAnAM, °kandare nivasatAM;
°kandarodaraBuvi</s> st. <s>°kandarezu
vasatAM</s>. ²b. <s>kaRAt</s> und <s>jalaM</s>
st. <s>kaRAn, eva</s> st. <s>aNke, SayAH</s>
st. <s>sTitAH</s>. ²c. <s>aparicita</s> und
<s>uparicita</s> st. <s>uparacita, prAcIna</s>
st. <s>prAsAda</s>. ²d. <s>maRqapa</s> st.
<s>kOtuka, puzAm</s> und <s>yuzAm</s> st.
<s>juzAm</s>.
</F>

heiligen Wortes ganz aufgehend, ihre
Jugend in einem Waldesdickicht des
besten der Berge verbringen; glücklich
sind aber auch diejenigen, welche am
Schlusse des Tages, die Geliebte, deren
Körper von der Last der hohen
strotzenden Brüste-Urnen erschöpft ist,
fest an sich drückend, auf weichem Lager
ruhen.

Fürsten sind hinterlistig, die Brahmanen
leben vom Waffenhandwerk, die Welt hängt
an den Weibern, die Weiber sind
leichtfertig, die Menschen fröhnen der
Gier, dem Guten geht es schlecht und der
Bösewicht schwimmt oben auf: aller
Wahrscheinlichkeit nach ist das
Zeitalter Kali eingetreten.

<s>nserzyaM mAravaDUBirityaBihito bOdDo jinaH pAtu vaH ..</s>
</S>
<D n="3173">
<b>3173.</b> Es behüte euch der Heilige der
Buddhisten, der einst von den Weibern
des Versuches also neidisch angeredet
wurde: an welche Jungfrau denkst du,
wenn du Vertiefung heuchelst und für
einen Augenblick dein Auge aufschlägst?
Sieh, obgleich man dich Erlöser nennt,
rettest du uns nicht, die wir durch des
Liebesgottes Pfeile verwundet sind. Mit
Unrecht nennt man dich den Barmherzigen;
wie könnte ein anderer Mann wohl
grausamer als du sein?
</D>

3173) PAÑCAT. ed. Bomb. V, 14. ²b.
<s>°SarAturaM janam</s> unsere Verbesserung
für <s>°SarAnuraYjanam</s>.

<s>na DyAtaM padamISvarasya viDivatsaMsAravicCittaye</s>
<s>svargadvArakapAwapAwanapawurDarmo 'pi nopArjitaH .</s>
<s>nArIpInapayoDaroruyugalaM svapne 'pi nAliNgitaM</s>
<s>mAtuH kevalameva yOvanavanacCede kuWArA vayam ..</s>
</S>
<D n="3318" a="1405">
<b>3318.</b> (<b>1405.</b>) Wir haben nicht auf
gehörige Weise auf Śiva's Stätte unsere
Gedanken gerichtet, wodurch der
Kreislauf des Lebens (die Wiedergeburt)
aufgehoben wird; auch haben wie keine
guten Werke eingesammelt, die geeignet
sind die Flügel des Himmelsthores
aufzureissen; auch haben wir selbst
nicht im Traume die vollen Brüste und
Hüften eines Weibes umfangen: wir sind
Nichts als die Axt, welche den Baum der
Jugend unserer Mutter niederhieb.
</D>
<F n="3318">
3318) BHARTṚ. ed. BOHL. 3, 46. HAEB.
und GALAN. 42. lith. Ausg. I 34, S. 30.
VṚDDHA-CĀṆ. 16, 1. SUBHĀṢ. 149. ²b.
<s>Darme</s>. ²b. und ²c. umgestellt. ²c.
<s>svanye</s> st. <s>svapne</s>. ²d. <s>vanaH</s>
und <s>vane</s> st. <s>vana</s>.

der Lohn von den Werken abhängt, was

Schicksal Nichts vermag!
